爱是地狱的恶狗：布考斯基诗集

2018-11-09 周五 by Bukowski

翻译说明

大概于2012年8月前译出初稿，2013年10月前做过一次修改。目前仍属未定稿。 这个诗集大概是美国读者评价最高的（参见bukowski.net的投票榜）。但根据我个人的感受，对中国读者的吸引力不如《弹醉琴》，也许是后者更粗糙有力，更符合中国读者的想象吧。

书名页

爱是地狱的恶狗/Love is a Dog from Hell 查尔斯·布考斯基/Charles Bukowski 诗歌 1974-1977/Poems 1974-1977

CCCO An Imprint of HarperCollinsPublishers

版权摘要

[1]帕蒂·赫斯特(Patty Hearst，1954–)，报业女继承人。全名Patricia Campbell Hearst，是威廉·伦道夫·赫斯特（William Randolph Hearst，1863–1951，美国报业与企业巨头，电影《公民凯恩》主角的原型）的孙女。1974年被共生解放军（Symbionese Liberation Army）绑架，洗脑后入伙，取名塔尼亚（Tania）。1975年被FBI找到，次年被起诉，以抢劫银行名义判了三年。2001年获得克林顿总统赦免。

疯狂/madness

1 我没有用拳头锤打四壁/I don't beat the walls with my fists 2 只是坐着/I just sit 3 可是它们冲过来/but it rushes in 4 势如潮水。/a tide of it.

5 院里住我后面那个女人天天晚上/the woman in the court behind me howls, 6 吼叫、哭泣。/weeps every night. 7 有时县里来人[1]/sometimes the county comes 8 把她带走一两天。/and takes her away for a day or two.

9 我以为她难过是因为丢失了/I believed she was suffering the loss 10 一次伟大的爱情/of a great love 11 直到有一天她过来跟我说起/until one day she came over and told me about 12 这件事——/it--- 13 他丢失了八套公寓房/she had lost 8 apartment houses 14 给一个软饭精——/to a gigolo who had swindled her out 15 把她给骗了。/of them. 16 她因为丢失财产又吼又哭。/she was howling and weeping over loss of property. 17 她一边对我开口一边哭起来/she began weeping as she told me 18 后来用描着旧唇膏/then with a mouth lined with stale lipstick 19 发出大蒜、洋葱味的嘴/and smelling of garlic and onions 20 吻我，说道：/she kissed me and told me: 21 “汉克，要是你没钱谁也不爱你。”/"Hank, nobody loves you if you don't have money."

22 她老了，差不多跟我一样老。/she's old, almost as old as I am.

23 她离开，还在哭泣……/she left, still weeping ...

24 前几天早上七点半两个黑人/the other morning at 7:30 a.m. two black 25 救护员抬着担架过来/attendants came with their stretcher, 26 但他们敲我的门。/only they knocked on my door.

27 “来吧，老兄，”高个儿的/"come on, man," said the tallest 28 对我说。/one.

29 “等等，”我说，“搞错了。”/"wait," I said, "there's a mistake."

30 我在可怕的宿醉中/I was terribly hungover 31 穿着撕破的浴袍站在/standing in my torn bathrobe 32 头发披散在眼前。/hair hanging down over my eyes.

五十六岁的诗人/a 56 year old poem

1 我和两位女士/I went with two ladies 2 去威尼斯[1]/down to Venice 3 找古董家具。/to look for antique furniture. 4 我把车停在商店后面/I parked in back of the store 5 然后和她们一起进去。/and went in with them. 6 一架钟一百二十五块，六把椅子七百，/$125 for a clock, $700 for 6 chairs. 7 我不看了。/I stopped looking.

8 女士们往前转/the ladies moved around 9 什么都瞧。/looking at everything. 10 女士们有品位。/the ladies had class. 11 我向其中一位招收告别/I waved goodbye to one of the ladies 12 然后出去。/and walked out.

13 那是星期天，酒吧/it was Sunday and the bar 14 很不好，/wasn't much better, 15 所有人都年轻且神经/everybody was nervous and young 16 白净，没有血色。/and blonde and pale. 17 我喝完酒，从酒水店/I finished my drink, got 4 beers 18 买了四瓶啤酒/at the liquor store 19 到车里喝。/and sat in my car drinking them.

20 喝完四瓶啤酒时/finishing the 4th beer 21 女士们出来了。/the ladies came out. 22 他们问我还好吗。/they asked me if I was all right. 23 我告诉她们所见所闻/I told them that every experience 24 都有些意思/meant something 25 她们已经把我从惯常的/and that they had pulled me out of 26 暗流中/my usual murky 27 拉出来。/current.

28 我最熟的那位花一百块/the one I knew best had bought a table 29 买了一张大理石台面的桌子。/with a marble top for $100. 30 她有自己的生意，是一位/she owned her own business and was a 31 文明人。/civilized person.

32 她文明得能够认识一位/she was civilized enough to know a neighbor 33 拥有篷车的邻居/who had a van 34 当我坐在她的公寓里喝/and while I sat in her apartment drinking 35 1974年的Zeller Schwarze Katz/1974 Zeller Schwarze Katz 36 她们下去搬那张桌子。/they went down and got the table.

37 后来她想知道我对那张桌子的/later she wanted to know what I thought about 38 想法，我说，我认为它没问题，/the table and I said I thought it was all right, 39 我有时在赛马场会输/sometimes I lost one hundred dollars at the 40 一百块。我们在床上看电视，后来/racetrack. we watched tv in bed and later 41 晚上我来不了[高潮]。我想是/that night I couldn't come. I think it was 42 因为我在想那张大理石桌子。/because I was thinking about that marble table. 43 我相信就是这样的。我家从来没有/I'm sure it was. 49 我确信那是个/I'm sure it's a giant 50 大骗局。/con.

年轻美女走过墓地/the beautiful young girl walking past the graveyard---

1 我在红绿灯前停下车/I stop my car at the signal 2 看见她走过墓地——/I see her walking past the graveyard---

3 她走过铁围栏时/as she walks past the iron fence 4 我能看穿铁围栏/I can see through the iron fence 5 看见墓石/and I see the headstones 6 和绿草地。/and the green lawn.

7 她的身体在铁围栏前运动/her body moves in front of the iron fence 8 墓石不动。/the headstones do not move.

9 我在想，/I think, 10 再没有别的人看见这景象吗？/doesn't anybody else see this?

11 我在想，/I think, 12 她看见那些墓石了吗？/does she see those headstones?

13 如果她看见了那么/if she does 14 她具有我所没有的智慧/she has wisdom that I don't have 15 因为她对它们似乎不予理睬。/for she appears to ignore them.

16 她的身体在自己神奇的/her body moving in its 17 液体中移动/magic fluid 18 她的长发被午后三点的太阳/and her long hair is lighted 19 照亮。/by the 3 p.m. sun.

20 红绿灯变了/the signal changes 21 她横过大街到西边/she crosses the street to the west 22 我向西开。/I drive west.

23 我把车开到海边/I drive my car down to the ocean 24 下车/get out 25 在大海面前/and run up and down 26 来回奔跑35分钟。/in front of the sea for 35 minutes 27 四处看到人/seeing people here and there 28 有眼睛有耳朵有脚趾/with eyes and ears and toes 29 和别的各种部件。/and various other parts.

30 好像谁也不在乎。/nobody seems to care.

15 他起身离开，带着一个十八岁的处女/he rose and left with an 18 year old virgin, the most 16 这些男女同校生中/beautiful co-ed of them 17 最美的一个。/all. 18 我合上笔记本/I closed my notebook 19 站起来跛足前行/got up and limped a 20 紧跟着/little bit behind 21 他们。/them.

金怀表/a gold pocket watch

1 我的祖父是个高个子德国人/my grandfather was a tall German 2 呼吸有一股怪味。/with a strange smell on his breath. 3 他笔直地站在/he stood very straight 4 自己的小房子前面/in front of his small house 5 他的妻子恨他/and his wife hated him 6 他的孩子认为他古怪。/and his children thought him odd. 7 我们第一次见面时我六岁/I was six the first time we met 8 他把自己所有的战斗勋章给了我/and he gave me all his war medals. 9 我第二次见他/the second time I met him 10 他把自己的金怀表给了我/he gave me his gold pocket watch. 11 它沉甸甸的，我拿回家/it was very heavy and I took it home 12 把它碰得很紧/and wound it very tight 13 不走了/and it stopped running 14 这让我难过。/which made me feel bad. 15 我再也没有见过他/I never saw him again 16 我的父母从不谈起他/and my parents never spoke of him 17 我的祖母也没有/nor did my grandmother 18 她很久以前/who had long ago 19 就不跟他一起生活。/stopped living with him. 20 有一次我问起他/once I asked about him 21 他们告诉我/and they told me 22 他太滥酒/he drank too much 23 但我最喜欢他/but I liked him best 24 笔直地站在/standing very straight 25 自己的房子前面/in front of his house 26 说，“哈喽，亨利，你/and saying, "hello, Henry, you 27 和我，我们彼此/and I, we know each 28 了解。”/other."

海滨旅行/beach trip

1 壮汉/the strong men 2 肌肉男/the muscle men 3 坐在那里/there they sit 4 在海边/down at the beach 5 可可粉的棕色/cocoa tans 6 赘肉/with the weights 7 散落四周/scattered about them 8 完好无损/untouched

9 他们坐着时/they sit as the 10 波浪涌来又/waves go in and 11 退去/out

16 他们坐着时/they sit while 17 碰一下纽扣/one punch of a button 18 就可能让他们的/could turn their 19 大鸡巴/turkeynecks to 20 变黑，火柴棍/black and shriveled 21 失效/matchsticks

22 他们坐着时/they sit while 23 演员休息室里在出卖自杀/suicides in green rooms 24 以换取空间/trade it in for space

25 他们坐着时以前的/they sit while former 26 美洲小姐/Miss Americas 27 在皱缩的镜子前/weep before wrinkled 28 哭泣/mirrors

29 他们坐着/they sit

30 他们坐着生命流/they sit with less 31 少于猿猴/life-flow than apes 32 我的女人停下/and my woman stops and 33 看他们：/looks at them: 34 “噢——噢——噢——”，她/"oooh oooh oooh," she 35 说。/says.

36 我带着我的女人/I walk off with 37 走开时波浪/my woman as the waves 38 涌来又退去。/go in and out.

39 “他们有点什么/"there's something wrong 40 问题，”她说，“是/with them," she said, "what 41 怎么回事？”/is it?"

42 “他们的爱只是/"their love only runs in 43 单向运行。”/one direction."

献给擦鞋男子的一首诗/one for the shoeshine man

1 攀爬圣莫尼卡悬崖的蜗牛们/the balance is preserved by the snails climbing the 2 所保持的叫平衡。/Santa Monica cliffs; 3 走在西大街上有按摩院的女孩/the luck is in walking down Western Avenue 4 向你喊，“哈喽，小甜甜！”/and having the girls in a massage 5 这叫幸运。/parlor holler at you, "Hello, Sweetie!" 6 五十五岁时有五个女人/the miracle is having 5 women in love 7 与你相爱叫奇迹，/with you at the age of 55, 8 你只能爱其中一个/and the goodness is that you are only able 9 那叫美德。/to love one of them. 10 有个女儿比你温柔/the gift is having a daughter more gentle 11 笑声比你美妙/than you are, whose laughter is finer 12 那叫礼物。/than yours. 13 开一辆67年的蓝色大众像少年郎/the peace comes from driving a 14 穿过街道，收音机调到/blue 67 Volks through the streets like a 15 《最爱你的老板娘》，感受阳光/teenager, radio tuned to The Host Who Loves You 16 感受新换马达稳定的哼唱/Most, feeling the sun, feeling the solid hum 17 穿行在车流中于是获得/of the rebuilt motor 18 平静。/as you needle through traffic. 19 还能喜欢摇滚乐，交响乐/the grace is being able to like rock music, 20 爵士……所有包含/symphony music, jazz ... 21 快乐原始能量的东西，/anything that contains the original energy of 22 这叫风度。/joy.

23 而旧病复发的可能在于/and the probability that returns 24 深蓝色的低潮/is the deep blue low 25 自己逼迫着自己/yourself flat upon yourself 26 身处断头台般的四壁中/within the guillotine walls 27 因电话响或者任何/angry at the sound of the phone 28 过路人的脚步声而生气。/or anybody's footsteps passing; 29 而另一个可能是——/but the other probability--- 30 轻快的高潮总是紧接而来——/the lilting high that always follows--- 31 让超市收银台的女孩/makes the girl at the checkstand in the 32 看起来像/supermarket look like 33 没有找到哈佛情人之前的/Marilyn 34 玛丽莲和杰姬/like Jackie before they got her Harvard lover 35 像我们回家都要跟踪的/like the girl in high school that we 36 高中女生。/all followed home.

37 有一种东西有助于你相信/there is that which helps you believe 38 死亡之外的东西——/in something else besides death: 39 街上一个人开车/somebody in a car approaching 40 靠你太近/on a street too narrow, 41 于是他或她开到一边让你/and he or she pulls aside to let you 42 通过，或者老拳手Beau Jack/by, or the old fighter Beau Jack 43 把钱撒光/shining shoes 44 在聚会上/after blowing the entire bankroll 45 在女人身上/on parties 46 在寄生虫身上/on women 47 然后去擦鞋/on parasites, 48 对着皮革上哼唱、哈气/humming, breathing on the leather, 49 捣鼓抹布/working the rag 50 抬头说：/looking up and saying: 51 “见鬼怎么回事，我弄了/"what the hell, I had it for a 52 好一阵。这还强过/while. that beats the 53 另一只。【？？】/other."

54 我有时感到辛酸/I am bitter sometimes 55 但滋味常是/but the taste has often been 56 甜美的。只是我/sweet. it's only that I've 57 怕说出来。这就像/feared to say it. it's like 58 当你的女人说/when your woman says, 59 “跟我说你爱我，”然而/"tell me you love me," and 60 你不能。/you can't.

61 如果你看见我在自己的/if you see me grinning from 62 大众车里嘻笑/my blue Volks 63 开过黄灯/running a yellow light 64 径直驶入阳光里/driving straight into the sun 65 那么我就是被疯狂生活的/I will be locked in the 66 双臂/arms of a 67 锁紧了/crazy life 68 心里想的是高空秋千演员/thinking of trapeze artists 69 抽大雪茄的侏儒/of midgets with big cigars 70 四十年代早期俄罗斯的冬天/of a Russian winter in the early 40's 71 携带着波兰泥土的肖邦。/of Chopin with his bag of Polish soil 72 一位老年女招待，笑着/of an old waitress bringing me an extra 73 拿给我额外/cup of coffee and laughing 74 一杯咖啡。/as she does so.

75 我喜欢你们之中最好的那些人/the best of you 76 比你们想象的还要喜欢。/I like more than you think. 77 别的人算不了什么/the others don't count 78 他们只是有指头有脑袋/except that they have fingers and heads 79 有些有眼睛/and some of them eyes 80 大多数有腿/and most of them legs 81 全部/and all of them 82 有美梦和噩梦/good and bad dreams 83 以及一条该走的路。/and a way to go.

84 公正无处不在，它正在起作用/justice is everywhere and it's working 85 机关枪、丑八怪/and the machine guns and the frogs 86 和隔离墙会告诉你【？？】/and the hedges will tell you 87 这一点。/so.
